ASSISTANT:      1→import React, { createContext, useContext, useState, useEffect, ReactNode } from 'react';
     2→import { auth, db } from '../utils/firebase';
     3→import { onAuthStateChanged } from 'firebase/auth';
     4→import { doc, getDoc } from 'firebase/firestore';
     5→
     6→interface UserData {
     7→  uid: string;
     8→  email: string;
     9→  firstName: string;
    10→  lastName: string;
    11→  name: string;
    12→  avatarUrl: string;
    13→  role: 'admin' | 'client';
    14→  status: string;
    15→}
    16→
    17→interface UserContextType {
    18→  user: UserData | null;
    19→  loading: boolean;
    20→  refreshUser: () => Promise<void>;
    21→}
    22→
    23→const UserContext = createContext<UserContextType | undefined>(undefined);
    24→
    25→export const UserProvider: React.FC<{ children: ReactNode }> = ({ children }) => {
    26→  const [user, setUser] = useState<UserData | null>(null);
    27→  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    28→
    29→  const fetchUserData = async (uid: string) => {
    30→    try {
    31→      // Force token refresh to ensure Firestore has valid credentials
    32→      const currentUser = auth.currentUser;
    33→      if (currentUser) {
    34→        await currentUser.getIdToken(true);
    35→      }
    36→
    37→      const userDocRef = doc(db, "users", uid);
    38→      const userDoc = await getDoc(userDocRef);
    39→
    40→      if (userDoc.exists()) {
    41→        const data = userDoc.data();
    42→        const authUser = auth.currentUser;
    43→
    44→        setUser({
    45→          uid,
    46→          email: authUser?.email || data.email || '',
    47→          firstName: data.firstName || '',
    48→          lastName: data.lastName || '',
    49→          name: data.name || `${data.firstName || ''} ${data.lastName || ''}`.trim(),
    50→          avatarUrl: data.avatarUrl || '',
    51→          role: data.role || 'client',
    52→          status: data.status || 'pending',
    53→        });
    54→      }
    55→    } catch {
    56→      // Auth state listener will handle re-authentication if needed
    57→    } finally {
    58→      setLoading(false);
    59→    }
    60→  };
    61→
    62→  const refreshUser = async () => {
    63→    const authUser = auth.currentUser;
    64→    if (authUser) {
    65→      await fetchUserData(authUser.uid);
    66→    }
    67→  };
    68→
    69→  useEffect(() => {
    70→    const unsubscribe = onAuthStateChanged(auth, async (authUser) => {
    71→      if (authUser) {
    72→        await fetchUserData(authUser.uid);
    73→      } else {
    74→        setUser(null);
    75→        setLoading(false);
    76→      }
    77→    });
    78→
    79→    return () => unsubscribe();
    80→  }, []);
    81→
    82→  return (
    83→    <UserContext.Provider value={{ user, loading, refreshUser }}>
    84→      {children}
    85→    </UserContext.Provider>
    86→  );
    87→};
    88→
    89→export const useUser = () => {
    90→  const context = useContext(UserContext);
    91→  if (context === undefined) {
    92→    throw new Error('useUser must be used within a UserProvider');
    93→  }
    94→  return context;
    95→};

ASSISTANT:      1→/**
     2→ * Removes keys with undefined values from an object before Firestore writes.
     3→ * Firestore rejects documents containing undefined field values.
     4→ */
     5→export function stripUndefined<T extends object>(obj: T): Partial<T> {
     6→  return Object.fromEntries(
     7→    Object.entries(obj).filter(([, v]) => v !== undefined)
     8→  ) as Partial<T>;
     9→}

'./UserContext';\nimport { toast } from 'sonner';\n\ninterface AdminContextType {\n  isAdminMode: boolean;\n  toggleAdminMode: () => void;\n  userRole: 'admin' | 'client';\n  isAdmin: boolean;\n  isLoadingAdminCheck: boolean;\n}\n\nconst AdminContext = createContext<AdminContextType | undefined>(undefined);\n\nexport const AdminProvider: React.FC<{ children: ReactNode }> = ({ children }) => {\n  const { user, loading } = useUser();\n  const navigate = useNavigate();\n  const location = useLocation();\n\n  // Load initial value from localStorage\n  const [isAdminMode, setIsAdminMode] = useState<boolean>(() => {\n    return localStorage.getItem('isAdminMode') === 'true';\n  });\n\n  // Derive admin status and role directly from UserContext\n  const userRole = user?.role || localStorage.setItem('isAdminMode', String(newValue));\n      return newValue;\n    });\n  };\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    try {\n      // If the user is fully loaded, is authenticated but NOT an admin...\n      if (!isLoadingAdminCheck && !isAdmin && user !== null) {\n        // ...and they attempt to access an admin-only path, reject and redirect.\n        if return (\n    <AdminContext.Provider\n      value={{\n        isAdminMode,\n        toggleAdminMode,\n        userRole,\n        isAdmin,\n        isLoadingAdminCheck,\n      }}\n    >\n      {children}\n    </AdminContext.Provider>\n  );\n};\n\nexport const useAdmin = (): AdminContextType => {\n  const context = useContext(AdminContext);\n  if (!context) {\n    throw new Error('useAdmin must be used within an AdminProvider');\n  }\n  return context;\n};\n"

     5→const router = Router();
     6→
     7→/**
     8→ * Middleware to check if Firebase Admin is initialized
     9→ * Returns 503 if not available
    10→ */
    11→function requireAdminSDK(req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction) {
    12→  if (!isAdminInitialized()) {
    13→    return res.status(503).json({
    14→      success: false,
    15→      error: 'Firebase Admin SDK not available. Service account not configured.'
    16→    });
    17→  }
    18→  next();
    19→}
    20→
    21→// Apply middleware to all admin routes
    22→router.use(requireAdminSDK);
    23→

    25→// USER MANAGEMENT ENDPOINTS

    28→/**
    29→ * Create a new user
    30→ * POST /admin/api/users
    31→ * Body: { email, password, displayName?, phoneNumber?, disabled? }
    32→ */
    33→router.post('/users', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
    34→  try {
    35→    const { email, password, displayName, phoneNumber, disabled } = req.body;
    36→
    37→    // Validate required fields
    38→    if (!email || !password) {
    39→      return res.status(400).json({
    40→        success: false,
    41→        error: 'Email and password are required'
    42→      });
    43→    }
    44→
    45→    // Create user with Firebase Auth
    46→    const userRecord = await getAuth().createUser({
    47→      email,
    48→      password,
    49→      displayName,
    50→      phoneNumber,
    51→      disabled: disabled || false
    52→    });
    53→
    54→    res.status(201).json({
    55→      success: true,
    56→      data: {
    57→        uid: userRecord.uid,
    58→        email: userRecord.email,
    59→        displayName: userRecord.displayName,
    60→        phoneNumber: userRecord.phoneNumber,
    61→        disabled: userRecord.disabled,
    62→        createdAt: userRecord.metadata.creationTime
    63→      }
    64→    });
    65→  } catch (error) {
    66→    logger.error({ err: error }, 'Error creating user');
    67→    res.status(500).json({
    68→      success: false,
    69→      error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to create user'
    70→    });
    71→  }
    72→});
    73→
    74→/**
    75→ * Get user by UID
    76→ * GET /admin/api/users/:uid
    77→ */
    78→router.get('/users/:uid', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
    79→  try {
    80→    const uid = req.params.uid as string;
    81→
    82→    const userRecord = await getAuth().getUser(uid);
    83→
    84→    res.json({
    85→      success: true,
    86→      data: {
    87→        uid: userRecord.uid,
    88→        email: userRecord.email || null,
    89→        displayName: userRecord.displayName || null,
    90→        phoneNumber: userRecord.phoneNumber || null,
    91→        photoURL: userRecord.photoURL || null,
    92→        disabled: userRecord.disabled,
    93→        emailVerified: userRecord.emailVerified,
    94→        customClaims: userRecord.customClaims || {},
    95→        createdAt: userRecord.metadata.creationTime,
    96→        lastSignInTime: userRecord.metadata.lastSignInTime || null
    97→      }
    98→    });
    99→  } catch (error) {
   100→    logger.error({ err: error }, 'Error getting user');
   101→    res.status(404).json({
   102→      success: false,
   103→      error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'User not found'
   104→    });
   105→  }
   106→});

   108→/**
   109→ * List users (paginated)
   110→ * GET /admin/api/users?limit=100&pageToken=xxx
   111→ */
   112→router.get('/users', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
   113→  try {
   114→    const limit = parseInt(req.query.limit as string) || 100;
   115→    const pageToken = req.query.pageToken as string | undefined;
   116→
   117→    const listUsersResult = await getAuth().listUsers(limit, pageToken);
   118→
   119→    res.json({
   120→      success: true,
   121→      data: {
   122→        users: listUsersResult.users.map(user => ({
   123→          uid: user.uid,
   124→          email: user.email,
   125→          displayName: user.displayName,
   126→          disabled: user.disabled,
   127→          emailVerified: user.emailVerified,
   128→          createdAt: user.metadata.creationTime
   129→        })),
   130→        pageToken: listUsersResult.pageToken
   131→      },
   132→      meta: {
   133→        total: listUsersResult.users.length,
   134→        hasMore: !!listUsersResult.pageToken
   135→      }
   136→    });
   137→  } catch (error) {
   138→    logger.error({ err: error }, 'Error listing users');
   139→    res.status(500).json({
   140→      success: false,
   141→      error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to list users'
   142→    });
   143→  }
   144→});

   146→/**
   147→ * Update user
   148→ * PUT /admin/api/users/:uid
   149→ * Body: { email?, displayName?, phoneNumber?, photoURL?, disabled? }
   150→ */
   151→router.put('/users/:uid', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
   152→  try {
   153→    const uid = req.params.uid as string;
   154→    const { email, displayName, phoneNumber, photoURL, disabled, password } = req.body;
   155→
   156→    const updateData: any = {};
   157→    if (email !== undefined) updateData.email = email;
   158→    if (displayName !== undefined) updateData.displayName = displayName;
   159→    if (phoneNumber !== undefined) updateData.phoneNumber = phoneNumber;
   160→    if (photoURL !== undefined) updateData.photoURL = photoURL;
   161→    if (disabled !== undefined) updateData.disabled = disabled;
   162→    if (password !== undefined) updateData.password = password;
   163→
   164→    const userRecord = await getAuth().updateUser(uid, updateData);
   165→
   166→    res.json({
   167→      success: true,
   168→      data: {
   169→        uid: userRecord.uid,
   170→        email: userRecord.email || null,
   171→        displayName: userRecord.displayName || null,
   172→        phoneNumber: userRecord.phoneNumber || null,
   173→        photoURL: userRecord.photoURL || null,
   174→        disabled: userRecord.disabled
   175→      }
   176→    });
   177→  } catch (error) {
   178→    logger.error({ err: error }, 'Error updating user');
   179→    res.status(500).json({
   180→      success: false,
   181→      error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to update user'
   182→    });
   183→  }
   184→});
   185→
   186→/**
   187→ * Delete user
   188→ * DELETE /admin/api/users/:uid
   189→ */
   190→router.delete('/users/:uid', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
   191→  try {
   192→    const uid = req.params.uid as string;
   193→
   194→    await getAuth().deleteUser(uid);
   195→

   197→      success: true,
   198→      data: { uid, deleted: true }
   199→    });
   200→  } catch (error) {
   201→    logger.error({ err: error }, 'Error deleting user');
   202→    res.status(500).json({
   203→      success: false,
   204→      error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to delete user'
   205→    });
   206→  }
   207→});
   208→
   209→/**
   210→ * Disable user account
   211→ * POST /admin/api/users/:uid/disable

   213→router.post('/users/:uid/disable', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {

   223→        disabled: userRecord.disabled

   236→ * Enable user account

   239→router.post('/users/:uid/enable', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
   240→  try {
   241→    const uid = req.params.uid as string;
   242→

   244→
   245→    res.json({
   246→      success: true,
   247→      data: {
   248→        uid: userRecord.uid,
   249→        disabled: userRecord.disabled

   266→ * Set custom claims on user (roles/permissions)
   267→ * POST /admin/api/users/:uid/claims
   268→ * Body: { claims: { admin: true, role: 'editor', ... } }
   269→ */
   270→router.post('/users/:uid/claims', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
   271→  try {
   272→    const uid = req.params.uid as string;
   273→    const { claims } = req.body;
   274→
   275→    if (!claims || typeof claims !== 'object') {
   276→      return res.status(400).json({
   277→        success: false,
   278→        error: 'Claims object is required'
   279→      });
   280→    }
   281→
   282→    await getAuth().setCustomUserClaims(uid, claims);
   283→
   284→    res.json({
   285→      success: true,
   286→      data: {
   287→        uid,
   288→        claims
   289→      }
   290→    });
   291→  } catch (error) {
   292→    logger.error({ err: error }, 'Error setting custom claims');
   293→    res.status(500).json({
   294→      success: false,

   296→    });
   297→  }
   298→});
   299→
   300→/**
   301→ * Get custom claims for user
   302→ * GET /admin/api/users/:uid/claims
   303→ */
   304→router.get('/users/:uid/claims', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
   305→  try {
   306→    const uid = req.params.uid as string;
   307→
   308→    const userRecord = await getAuth().getUser(uid);
   309→
   310→    res.json({
   311→      success: true,
   312→      data: {
   313→        uid,
   314→        claims: userRecord.customClaims || {}
   315→      }
   316→    });
   317→  } catch (error) {
   318→    logger.error({ err: error }, 'Error getting custom claims');
   319→    res.status(404).json({
   320→      success: false,
   321→      error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'User not found'
   322→    });
   323→  }
   324→});
   325→
   326→// ============================================================================
   327→// BULK OPERATIONS ENDPOINTS
   328→// ============================================================================
   329→
   330→/**
   331→ * Bulk import users
   332→ * POST /admin/api/bulk/users/import
   333→ * Body: { users: [{ email, password, displayName?, ... }] }
   334→ */
   335→router.post('/bulk/users/import', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
   336→  try {
   337→    const { users } = req.body;
   338→
   339→    if (!Array.isArray(users) || users.length === 0) {
   340→      return res.status(400).json({
   341→        success: false,
   342→        error: 'Users array is required'
   343→      });
   344→    }
   345→
   346→    const results = await Promise.allSettled(
   347→      users.map(userData => getAuth().createUser(userData))
   348→    );
   349→
   350→    const successful = results.filter(r => r.status === 'fulfilled').length;
   351→    const failed = results.filter(r => r.status === 'rejected').length;
   352→
   353→    res.json({
   354→      success: true,
   355→      data: {
   356→        total: users.length,
   357→        successful,
   358→        failed,
   359→        results: results.map((r, idx) => ({
   360→          index: idx,
   361→          status: r.status,
   362→          uid: r.status === 'fulfilled' ? r.value.uid : null,
   363→          error: r.status === 'rejected' ? r.reason.message : null
   364→        }))
   365→      }
   366→    });
   367→  } catch (error) {
   368→    logger.error({ err: error }, 'Error importing users');
   369→    res.status(500).json({
   370→      success: false,
   371→      error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to import users'
   372→    });
   373→  }
   374→});
   375→
   376→/**
   377→ * Bulk export users
   378→ * GET /admin/api/bulk/users/export?limit=1000
   379→ */
   380→router.get('/bulk/users/export', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
   381→  try {
   382→    const limit = parseInt(req.query.limit as string) || 1000;
   383→    const allUsers: any[] = [];
   384→    let pageToken: string | undefined = undefined;
   385→
   386→    // Paginate through all users
   387→    do {
   388→      const listUsersResult = await getAuth().listUsers(1000, pageToken);
   389→      allUsers.push(...listUsersResult.users.map(user => ({
   390→        uid: user.uid,
   391→        email: user.email,
   392→        displayName: user.displayName,
   393→        phoneNumber: user.phoneNumber,
   394→        disabled: user.disabled,
   395→        emailVerified: user.emailVerified,
   396→        customClaims: user.customClaims,
   397→        createdAt: user.metadata.creationTime,
   398→        lastSignInTime: user.metadata.lastSignInTime
   399→      })));
   400→      pageToken = listUsersResult.pageToken;
   401→
   402→      if (allUsers.length >= limit) break;
   403→    } while (pageToken);
   404→
   405→    res.json({
   406→      success: true,
   407→      data: {
   408→        users: allUsers.slice(0, limit),
   409→        total: allUsers.length,
   410→        exportedAt: new Date().toISOString()
   411→      }
   412→    });
   413→  } catch (error) {
   414→    logger.error({ err: error }, 'Error exporting users');
   415→    res.status(500).json({
   416→      success: false,
   417→      error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to export users'
   418→    });
   419→  }
   420→});
   421→
   422→/**
   423→ * Backup Firestore collection
   424→ * POST /admin/api/bulk/firestore/backup
   425→ * Body: { collection: 'collectionName' }
   426→ */
   427→router.post('/bulk/firestore/backup', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
   428→  try {
   429→    const { collection } = req.body;
   430→
   431→    if (!collection) {
   432→      return res.status(400).json({
   433→        success: false,
   434→        error: 'Collection name is required'
   435→      });
   436→    }
   437→
   438→    const snapshot = await getFirestore().collection(collection).get();
   439→    const documents = snapshot.docs.map(doc => ({
   440→      id: doc.id,
   441→      data: doc.data()
   442→    }));
   443→
   444→    res.json({
   445→      success: true,
   446→      data: {
   447→        collection,
   448→        documents,
   449→        count: documents.length,
   450→        backedUpAt: new Date().toISOString()
   451→      }
   452→    });
   453→  } catch (error) {
   454→    logger.error({ err: error }, 'Error backing up collection');
   455→    res.status(500).json({
   456→      success: false,
   457→      error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to backup collection'
   458→    });
   459→  }
   460→});
   461→
   462→/**
   463→ * Restore Firestore collection
   464→ * POST /admin/api/bulk/firestore/restore
   465→ * Body: { collection: 'collectionName', documents: [{ id, data }, ...] }
   466→ */
   467→router.post('/bulk/firestore/restore', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
   468→  try {
   469→    const { collection, documents } = req.body;
   470→
   471→    if (!collection || !Array.isArray(documents)) {
   472→      return res.status(400).json({
   473→        success: false,
   474→        error: 'Collection name and documents array are required'
   475→      });
   476→    }
   477→
   478→    const batch = getFirestore().batch();
   479→    documents.forEach(doc => {
   480→      const docRef = getFirestore().collection(collection).doc(doc.id);
   481→      batch.set(docRef, doc.data);
   482→    });
   483→
   484→    await batch.commit();
   485→
   486→    res.json({
   487→      success: true,
   488→      data: {
   489→        collection,
   490→        restored: documents.length,
   491→        restoredAt: new Date().toISOString()
   492→      }
   493→    });
   494→  } catch (error) {
   495→    logger.error({ err: error }, 'Error restoring collection');
   496→    res.status(500).json({
   497→      success: false,
   498→      error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to restore collection'
   499→    });
   500→  }
   501→});
   502→
   503→export default router;
   504→

ASSISTANT:      1→import express from 'express';
     2→import helmet from 'helmet';
     3→import cors from 'cors';
     4→import rateLimit from 'express-rate-limit';
     5→import dotenv from 'dotenv';
     6→import path from 'path';
     7→import logger from './logger';
     8→dotenv.config({ path: path.resolve(__dirname, '../.env') });
     9→import proxyHandler from './proxy';
    10→import { optionalApiKeyAuth } from './authMiddleware';

    22→
    23→// Trust proxy - Single nginx reverse proxy

    25→
    26→// Security middleware - Helmet for security headers
    27→app.use(helmet({
    28→  contentSecurityPolicy: false, // Disabled because proxy modifies CSP
    29→  crossOriginEmbedderPolicy: false, // Allow embedding
    30→}));
    31→
    32→// CORS configuration - Strict origin validation in production
    33→const PRODUCTION_DEFAULT_ORIGINS = ['https://client.samixism.com', 'http://client.samixism.com'];
    34→
    35→const allowedOrigins = process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS
    36→  ? process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS.split(',').map(o => o.trim()).filter(Boolean)
    37→  : (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production'
    38→      ? PRODUCTION_DEFAULT_ORIGINS // Fallback to known production origins instead of crashing
    39→      : ['http://localhost:3000', 'http://localhost:5173']); // Dev mode only
    40→
    41→if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' && !process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS) {
    42→  // Warn loudly in logs but DO NOT crash — PM2 will just restart into a crash loop
    43→  logger.warn({ fallbackOrigins: PRODUCTION_DEFAULT_ORIGINS }, 'ALLOWED_ORIGINS env var not set — using hardcoded fallback');
    44→}
    45→
    46→app.use(cors({
    47→  origin: (origin, callback) => {
    48→    // Allow requests with no origin (mobile apps, Postman, etc.)
    49→    if (!origin) return callback(null, true);
    50→
    51→    if (allowedOrigins.includes(origin)) {
    52→      callback(null, true);
    53→    } else {
    54→      logger.warn({ origin }, 'Blocked CORS request from unauthorized origin');
    55→      callback(new Error('CORS policy violation'));
    56→    }
    57→  },
    58→  methods: ['GET', 'POST', 'PUT', 'DELETE', 'OPTIONS'],
    59→  credentials: true,
    60→}));
    61→
    62→// Health check endpoints (BEFORE rate limiter to avoid blocking monitoring)
    63→// Health check endpoint for load balancer and monitoring
    64→app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
    65→  const healthcheck = {
    66→    uptime: process.uptime(),
    67→    message: 'OK',
    68→    timestamp: Date.now(),
    69→    service: 'client-dashboard-api',
    70→    version: process.env.npm_package_version || '1.0.0',
    71→  };
    72→
    73→  try {
    74→    res.status(200).json(healthcheck);
    75→  } catch (error) {
    76→    healthcheck.message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error';
    77→    res.status(503).json(healthcheck);
    78→  }
    79→});
    80→
    81→// Readiness check (for Kubernetes-style orchestration)
    82→app.get('/ready', (req, res) => {
    83→  // Add checks for database connections, external services, etc.
    84→  const ready = {
    85→    ready: true,
    86→    timestamp: Date.now(),

    96→});
    97→
    98→// Liveness check (minimal check that process is alive)
    99→app.get('/alive', (req, res) => {
   100→  res.status(200).json({ alive: true });
   101→});
   102→
   103→// Rate limiting - Prevent abuse
   104→const limiter = rateLimit({
   105→  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
   106→  max: process.env.RATE_LIMIT_MAX ? parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_MAX) : 100, // 100 requests per windowMs
   107→  message: { error: 'Too many requests, please try again later.' },
   108→  standardHeaders: true,
   109→  legacyHeaders: false,
   110→});
   111→

   113→
   114→// Parse JSON bodies with size limit
   115→app.use(express.json({ limit: '1mb' }));
   116→app.use(express.urlencoded({ limit: '1mb', extended: true }));
   117→
   118→// VercelRequest and VercelResponse are compatible enough with Express req/res
   119→// for the purposes of our proxyHandler. A small adapter might be needed if we add complexity.
   120→app.get('/api/proxy', optionalApiKeyAuth, (req, res) => {
   121→  proxyHandler(req, res);
   122→});
   123→
   124→// AI helper endpoints (backend-only secrets)
   125→// 1) Extract colors from text (best-effort hex color extraction for dev)
   126→app.post('/api/ai/extract-colors', (req, res) => {
   127→  const { text } = req.body;
   128→  if (!text || typeof text !== 'string') {
   129→    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Text content required' });
   130→  }
   131→  // Simple fallback: extract hex color codes from text
   132→  const hexes = (text.match(/#([0-9a-fA-F]{3}|[0-9a-fA-F]{6})/g) || []).slice(0, 20);
   133→  const colors = hexes.map(h => ({ name: h, hex: h }));
   134→  res.json({ colors });
   135→});
   136→
   137→// 2) Generate a brand asset (image) using AI on the backend
   138→app.post('/api/ai/generate-brand-asset', async (req, res) => {
   139→  const { logoUrl, prompt } = req.body;
   140→  if (!logoUrl || !prompt) {
   141→    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'logoUrl and prompt are required' });
   142→  }
   143→  // In a full deployment, this would call Google GenAI or another AI service using a secret key kept on the server.
   144→  // For now, return a lightweight placeholder image data URL to keep the flow working in development.
   145→  const placeholder = 'data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVR4nGNgYAAAAAMAASsJTYQAAAAASUVORK5CYII=';
   146→  return res.json({ imageUrl: placeholder });
   147→});
   148→
   149→// Novu notifications API
   150→app.use('/api/notifications', notificationsRouter);
   151→
   152→// Social media API (OAuth + platform data proxy)
   153→app.use('/api/social', socialRouter);
   154→
   155→// Webhook handlers (Instagram, Facebook, Twitter, etc.)
   156→app.use('/api/webhooks', webhookRouter);
   157→

   159→app.use('/admin/api', optionalApiKeyAuth, adminRouter);
   160→
   161→// Paymenter billing & subscription proxy
   162→app.use('/api/paymenter', paymenterRouter);
   163→
   164→// Google Drive file manager
   165→app.use('/api/drive', driveRouter);
   166→
   167→// Meilisearch search proxy (keeps master key server-side)
   168→app.use('/api/search', optionalApiKeyAuth, searchRouter);
   169→
   170→export { app };
   171→
   172→if (require.main === module) {
   173→  app.listen(port, () => {
   174→    logger.info({ port }, 'API server listening');
   175→
   176→    // PM2 ready signal — MUST be sent AFTER listen() confirms port is bound
   177→    // Sending it before listen() causes PM2 cluster reload race conditions
   178→    if (process.send) {
   179→      process.send('ready');
   180→    }
   181→  });
   182→}

ASSISTANT:      1→import { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';
     2→import logger from './logger';
     3→
     4→/**
     5→ * API Key authentication middleware
     6→ * REQUIRED in production, optional in development
     7→ */
     8→export function optionalApiKeyAuth(req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction) {
     9→  const expectedApiKey = process.env.API_KEY;
    10→
    11→  // In production, API_KEY is REQUIRED
    12→  if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' && !expectedApiKey) {
    13→    logger.error('API_KEY environment variable is required in production');
    14→    return res.status(500).json({
    15→      error: 'Server configuration error. Contact administrator.'
    16→    });
    17→  }
    18→
    19→  // If no API_KEY is configured in development, skip authentication (backward compatible)
    20→  if (!expectedApiKey && process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
    21→    logger.warn('API running without authentication in development mode');
    22→    return next();
    23→  }
    24→
    25→  // If API_KEY is configured, require it in the request
    26→  const providedApiKey = req.headers['x-api-key'] || req.query.apiKey;
    27→
    28→  if (!providedApiKey) {
    29→    return res.status(401).json({
    30→      error: 'API key required. Provide it via X-API-Key header or apiKey query parameter.'
    31→    });
    32→  }
    33→
    34→  if (providedApiKey !== expectedApiKey) {
    35→    return res.status(403).json({
    36→      error: 'Invalid API key'
    37→    });
    38→  }
    39→
    40→  next();
    41→}
    42→

    11→ *
    12→ * Service account key location:

    17→// Singleton instance
    18→let adminApp: admin.app.App | null = null;
    19→let isInitialized = false;
    20→
    21→/**
    22→ * Initialize Firebase Admin SDK
    23→ * @returns Firebase Admin app instance or null if initialization fails
    24→ */
    25→export function initializeFirebaseAdmin(): admin.app.App | null {
    26→  // Return existing instance if already initialized
    27→  if (adminApp) {
    28→    return adminApp;
    29→  }
    30→
    31→  try {
    32→    // If in test environment, initialize with a dummy project ID
    33→    if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'test') {
    34→      adminApp = admin.initializeApp({ projectId: 'demo-test' });
    35→      isInitialized = true;
    36→      logger.info('Firebase Admin SDK initialized in TEST mode');
    37→      return adminApp;
    38→    }
    39→
    40→    // Determine service account path
    41→    const serviceAccountPath = process.env.FIREBASE_SERVICE_ACCOUNT_PATH ||
    42→      '/home/clientdash/.firebase-admin.json';
    43→
    44→    // Check if service account file exists
    45→    if (!fs.existsSync(serviceAccountPath)) {
    46→      logger.warn({ serviceAccountPath }, 'Firebase Admin SDK: service account not found');
    47→      logger.warn('Admin API endpoints will return 503 Service Unavailable');
    48→      return null;
    49→    }
    50→
    51→    // Read and parse service account
    52→    const serviceAccount = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(serviceAccountPath, 'utf8'));
    53→
    54→    // Initialize Firebase Admin
    55→    adminApp = admin.initializeApp({
    56→      credential: admin.credential.cert(serviceAccount),
    57→      databaseURL: "https://client-dashboard-v2-default-rtdb.europe-west1.firebasedatabase.app"
    58→    });
    59→
    60→    isInitialized = true;
    61→    logger.info({ projectId: serviceAccount.project_id, serviceAccount: serviceAccount.client_email }, 'Firebase Admin SDK initialized');
    62→
    63→    return adminApp;
    64→  } catch (error) {
    65→    logger.error({ err: error }, 'Firebase Admin SDK initialization failed — admin endpoints will return 503');
    66→    return null;
    67→  }
    68→}

Try again later.' },\n});\n\n/**\n * Admin auth middleware.\n *\n * Flow:\n * 1. Check Firebase Admin SDK is initialized (503 if not)\n * 2. Extract Bearer token from Authorization header\n *    → 401 { success: false, error: 'Authorization header required' } if missing\n * 3. verifyIdToken(token, true)  ← checkRevoked=true\n *    → 401 { success: false, error: 'Invalid or expired token' } on failure\n * 4. Fetch Firestore doc users/{uid}\n *    → 403 { success: false, error: 'Admin access required' } if doc missing or role !== 'admin'\n * 5. Attach req.adminUser = { uid, email, role }\n * 6. Write failure events to adminAuditLog collection (best-effort, never block request)\n * 7. Call next()\n */\nexport async function adminAuthMiddleware(req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction): Promise<void> {\n  // 1. SDK check\n  if (!isAdminInitialized()) {\n    res.status(503).json({ success: false, error: 'Firebase Admin SDK not available.' });\n    return;\n  }\n\n  const authHeader = req.headers['authorization'];\n\n  // 2. Extract token\n  if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {\n    await writeAuditLog('missing_token', null, req);\n    res.status(401).json({ success: false, error: 'Authorization header required. Use: Bearer <token>' });\n    return;\n  }\n\n  const token = authHeader.slice(7); // remove 'Bearer '\n\n  let uid: string;\n  let email: string;\n\n  try {\n    // 3. Verify token (checkRevoked = true for security)\n    const decodedToken = await getAuth().verifyIdToken(token, true);\n    uid = decodedToken.uid;\n    email = decodedToken.email ?? '';\n  } catch (error) {\n    logger.warn({ err: error }, 'Admin auth: token verification failed');\n    await writeAuditLog('invalid_token', null, req);\n    res.status(401).json({ success: false, error: 'Invalid or expired token.' });\n    return;\n  }\n\n  try {\n    // 4. Check Firestore role\n    const userDoc = await getFirestore().collection('users').doc(uid).get();\n\n    if (!userDoc.exists) {\n      logger.warn({ uid }, 'Admin auth: user doc not found in Firestore');\n      await writeAuditLog('user_not_found', uid, req);\n      res.status(403).json({ success: false, error: 'Admin access required.' });\n      return;\n    }\n\n    const data = userDoc.data()!;\n    const role: string = data.role ?? 'client';\n\n    if (role !== 'admin') {\n      logger.warn({ uid, role }, 'Admin auth: non-admin user attempted access');\n      await writeAuditLog('not_admin', uid, req);\n      res.status(403).json({ success: false, error: 'Admin access required.' });\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // 5. Attach to request\n    req.adminUser = { uid, email, role };\n    next();\n\n  } catch (error) {\n    logger.error({ err: error, uid }, 'Admin auth: Firestore role check failed');\n    await writeAuditLog('firestore_error', uid, req);\n    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: 'Authentication check failed.' });\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Best-effort write to adminAuditLog. Never throws — failures are logged and swallowed.\n */\nasync function writeAuditLog(reason: string, uid: string | null, req: Request): Promise<void> {\n  try {\n    await getFirestore().collection('adminAuditLog').add({\n      event: 'auth_failure',\n      reason,\n      uid,\n      ip: req.ip ?? null,\n      method: req.method,\n      path: req.path,\n      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),\n    });\n  } catch (err) {\n    logger.warn({ err }, 'adminAuthMiddleware: failed to write audit log');\n  }\n}\n```\n\nWrite EXACTLY this to `C:\\Users\\Sami\\client-dashboard\\api\\adminAuthMiddleware.ts`. JSON.stringify(body) : undefined,\n      });\n\n      const json: ApiResponse<T> = await res.json();\n\n      if (!res.ok || !json.success) {\n        const message = json.error ?? `Request failed: ${res.status} ${res.statusText}`;\n        toast.error(message);\n        return null;\n      }\n\n      return (json.data ?? null) as T | null;\n    } catch (err) {\n      const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Network error';\n      toast.error(message);\n      return null;\n    } finally {\n      setLoading(false);\n    }\n  }, [buildHeaders]);\n\n  const get = useCallback(<T>(\n    path: string,\n    params?: Record<string, string | number | boolean>\n  ) => request<T>('GET', path, undefined, params), [request]);\n\n  const post = useCallback(<T>(path: string, body: unknown) =>\n    request<T>('POST', path, body), [request]);\n\n  const put = useCallback(<T>(path: string, body: unknown) =>\n    request<T>('PUT', path, body), [request]);\n\n  const patch = useCallback(<T>(path: string, body: unknown) =>\n    request<T>('PATCH', path, body), [request]);\n\n  const del = useCallback(<T>(path: string, body?: unknown) =>\n    request<T>('DELETE', path, body), [request]);\n\n  const bulkDelete = useCallback(<T>(path: string, ids: string[]) =>\n    request<T>('DELETE', path, { ids }), [request]);\n\n  return { loading, get, post, put, patch, del, bulkDelete };\n}\n```\n\nWrite EXACTLY this content to `C:\\Users\\Sami\\client-dashboard\\hooks\\useAdminApi.ts`. Try again later.' },\n});\n\n/**\n * Admin auth middleware.\n *\n * Flow:\n * 1. Check Firebase Admin SDK is initialized (503 if not)\n * 2. Extract Bearer token from Authorization header\n *    → 401 { success: false, error: 'Authorization header required' } if missing\n * 3. verifyIdToken(token, true)  ← checkRevoked=true\n *    → 401 { success: false, error: 'Invalid or expired token' } on failure\n * 4. Fetch Firestore doc users/{uid}\n *    → 403 { success: false, error: 'Admin access required' } if doc missing or role !== 'admin'\n * 5. Attach req.adminUser = { uid, email, role }\n * 6. Write failure events to adminAuditLog collection (best-effort, never block request)\n * 7. Call next()\n */\nexport async function adminAuthMiddleware(req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction): Promise<void> {\n  // 1. SDK check\n  if (!isAdminInitialized()) {\n    res.status(503).json({ success: false, error: 'Firebase Admin SDK not available.' });\n    return;\n  }\n\n  const authHeader = req.headers['authorization'];\n\n  // 2. Extract token\n  if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {\n    await writeAuditLog('missing_token', null, req);\n    res.status(401).json({ success: false, error: 'Authorization header required. Use: Bearer <token>' });\n    return;\n  }\n\n  const token = authHeader.slice(7); // remove 'Bearer '\n\n  let uid: string;\n  let email: string;\n\n  try {\n    // 3. Verify token (checkRevoked = true for security)\n    const decodedToken = await getAuth().verifyIdToken(token, true);\n    uid = decodedToken.uid;\n    email = decodedToken.email ?? '';\n  } catch (error) {\n    logger.warn({ err: error }, 'Admin auth: token verification failed');\n    await writeAuditLog('invalid_token', null, req);\n    res.status(401).json({ success: false, error: 'Invalid or expired token.' });\n    return;\n  }\n\n  try {\n    // 4. Check Firestore role\n    const userDoc = await getFirestore().collection('users').doc(uid).get();\n\n    if (!userDoc.exists) {\n      logger.warn({ uid }, 'Admin auth: user doc not found in Firestore');\n      await writeAuditLog('user_not_found', uid, req);\n      res.status(403).json({ success: false, error: 'Admin access required.' });\n      return;\n    }\n\n    const data = userDoc.data()!;\n    const role: string = data.role ?? 'client';\n\n    if (role !== 'admin') {\n      logger.warn({ uid, role }, 'Admin auth: non-admin user attempted access');\n      await writeAuditLog('not_admin', uid, req);\n      res.status(403).json({ success: false, error: 'Admin access required.' });\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // 5. Attach to request\n    req.adminUser = { uid, email, role };\n    next();\n\n  } catch (error) {\n    logger.error({ err: error, uid }, 'Admin auth: Firestore role check failed');\n    await writeAuditLog('firestore_error', uid, req);\n    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: 'Authentication check failed.' });\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Best-effort write to adminAuditLog. Never throws — failures are logged and swallowed.\n */\nasync function writeAuditLog(reason: string, uid: string | null, req: Request): Promise<void> {\n  try {\n    await getFirestore().collection('adminAuditLog').add({\n      event: 'auth_failure',\n      reason,\n      uid,\n      ip: req.ip ?? null,\n      method: req.method,\n      path: req.path,\n      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),\n    });\n  } catch (err) {\n    logger.warn({ err }, 'adminAuthMiddleware: failed to write audit log');\n  }\n}\n```\n\nWrite EXACTLY this to `C:\\Users\\Sami\\client-dashboard\\api\\adminAuthMiddleware.ts`. Please sign in.');\n      return null;\n    }\n    try {\n      // forceRefresh=false — Firebase SDK auto-refreshes if expired\n      return await currentUser.getIdToken(false);\n    } catch {\n      toast.error('Session expired. Please sign in again.');\n      return null;\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  /** Build headers with Authorization token */\n  const buildHeaders = useCallback(async (includeBody = false): Promise<HeadersInit | null> => {\n    const token = await getToken();\n    if (!token) return null;\n    const headers: HeadersInit = {\n      'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}`,\n    };\n    if (includeBody) headers['Content-Type'] = 'application/json';\n    return headers;\n  }, [getToken]);\n\n  /** Core fetch wrapper */\n  const request = useCallback(async <T>(\n    method: string,\n    path: string,\n    body?: unknown,\n    params?: Record<string, string | number | boolean>\n  ): Promise<T | null> => {\n    setLoading(true);\n    try {\n      const headers = await buildHeaders(body !== undefined);\n      if (!headers) return null; // auth failed, toast already shown\n\n      let url = `${BASE_URL}${path.startsWith('/') ? path : '/' + path}`;\n      if (params && Object.keys(params).length > 0) {\n        const qs = new URLSearchParams(\n          Object.fromEntries(Object.entries(params).map(([k, v]) => [k, String(v)]))\n        ).toString();\n        url += `?${qs}`;\n      }\n\n      const res = await fetch(url, {\n        method,\n        headers,\n        body: body !== undefined ? JSON.stringify(body) : undefined,\n      });\n\n      const json: ApiResponse<T> = await res.json();\n\n      if (!res.ok || !json.success) {\n        const message = json.error ?? `Request failed: ${res.status} ${res.statusText}`;\n        toast.error(message);\n        return null;\n      }\n\n      return (json.data ?? null) as T | null;\n    } catch (err) {\n      const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Network error';\n      toast.error(message);\n      return null;\n    } finally {\n      setLoading(false);\n    }\n  }, [buildHeaders]);\n\n  const get = useCallback(<T>(\n    path: string,\n    params?: Record<string, string | number | boolean>\n  ) => request<T>('GET', path, undefined, params), [request]);\n\n  const post = useCallback(<T>(path: string, body: unknown) =>\n    request<T>('POST', path, body), [request]);\n\n  const put = useCallback(<T>(path: string, body: unknown) =>\n    request<T>('PUT', path, body), [request]);\n\n  const patch = useCallback(<T>(path: string, body: unknown) =>\n    request<T>('PATCH', path, body), [request]);\n\n  const del = useCallback(<T>(path: string, body?: unknown) =>\n    request<T>('DELETE', path, body), [request]);\n\n  const bulkDelete = useCallback(<T>(path: string, ids: string[]) =>\n    request<T>('DELETE', path, { ids }), [request]);\n\n  return { loading, get, post, put, patch, del, bulkDelete };\n}\n```\n\nWrite EXACTLY this content to `C:\\Users\\Sami\\client-dashboard\\hooks\\useAdminApi.ts`. Please sign in.');\n      return null;\n    }\n    try {\n      return await currentUser.getIdToken(false);\n    } catch {\n      toast.error('Session expired. Please sign in again.');\n      return null;\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  const buildHeaders = useCallback(\n    async (includeBody = false): Promise<HeadersInit | null> => {\n      const token = await getToken();\n      if (!token) return null;\n      const headers: HeadersInit = { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` };\n      if (includeBody) headers['Content-Type'] = 'application/json';\n      return headers;\n    },\n    [getToken]\n  );\n\n  const request = useCallback(\n    async <T>(\n      method: string,\n      path: string,\n      body?: unknown,\n      params?: Record<string, string | number | boolean>\n    ): Promise<T | null> => {\n      setLoading(true);\n      try {\n        const headers = await buildHeaders(body !== undefined);\n        if (!headers) return null;\n\n        let url = `${BASE_URL}${path.startsWith('/') ? path : '/' + path}`;\n        if (params && Object.keys(params).length > 0) {\n          const qs = new URLSearchParams(\n            Object.fromEntries(Object.entries(params).map(([k, v]) => [k, String(v)]))\n          ).toString();\n          url += `?${qs}`;\n        }\n\n        const res = await fetch(url, {\n          method,\n          headers,\n          body: body !== undefined ? JSON.stringify(body) : undefined,\n        });\n\n        const json: ApiResponse<T> = await res.json();\n\n        if (!res.ok || !json.success) {\n          const message = json.error ?? `Request failed: ${res.status} ${res.statusText}`;\n          toast.error(message);\n          return null;\n        }\n\n        return (json.data ?? null) as T | null;\n      } catch (err) {\n        toast.error(err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Network error');\n        return null;\n      } finally {\n        setLoading(false);\n      }\n    },\n    [buildHeaders]\n  );\n\n  const get = useCallback(\n    <T>(path: string, params?: Record<string, string | number | boolean>) =>\n      request<T>('GET', path, undefined, params),\n    [request]\n  );\n\n  const post = useCallback(\n    <T>(path: string, body: unknown) => request<T>('POST', path, body),\n    [request]\n  );\n\n  const put = useCallback(\n    <T>(path: string, body: unknown) => request<T>('PUT', path, body),\n    [request]\n  );\n\n  const patch = useCallback(\n    <T>(path: string, body: unknown) => request<T>('PATCH', path, body),\n    [request]\n  );\n\n  const del = useCallback(\n    <T>(path: string, body?: unknown) => request<T>('DELETE', path, body),\n    [request]\n  );\n\n  const bulkDelete = useCallback(\n    <T>(path: string, ids: string[]) => request<T>('DELETE', path, { ids }),\n    [request]\n  );\n\n  return { loading, get, post, put, patch, del, bulkDelete };\n}\n```\n\nUse the Write tool to create this file at the exact path specified. ASSISTANT: The file has been created at `C:\Users\Sami\client-dashboard\api\adminAuthMiddleware.ts`.

The file contains:

- **`adminRateLimiter`** - An `express-rate-limit` middleware configured for 100 requests per 15 minutes per IP, with standard headers enabled and a structured JSON error message.

- **`adminAuthMiddleware`** - An async Express middleware that performs a 7-step admin authentication chain:
  1. Checks Firebase Admin SDK initialization (503 if unavailable)
  2. Validates the `Authorization: Bearer <token>` header (401 if missing)
  3. Calls `verifyIdToken(token, true)` with revocation checking (401 on failure)
  4. Fetches `users/{uid}` from Firestore and verifies `role === 'admin'` (403 if not)
  5. Attaches `req.adminUser = { uid, email, role }` for downstream handlers
  6. Writes all auth failures to `adminAuditLog` collection (best-effort, never blocks)
  7. Calls `next()`

- **`writeAuditLog`** - A private best-effort helper that logs failure events (reason, uid, IP, method, path, timestamp) to Firestore's `adminAuditLog` collection without ever throwing.

- **Global Express type augmentation** - Extends `Express.Request` with the optional `adminUser` field so TypeScript compiles cleanly across the codebase.

The file is a React hook that provides a typed, authenticated HTTP client for Admin CMS API calls. Key aspects of what was written:

- **Authentication**: Automatically fetches and injects the Firebase ID token as `Authorization: Bearer <token>` on every request via `getToken` and `buildHeaders`.
- **Methods exposed**: `get`, `post`, `put`, `patch`, `del`, and `bulkDelete` — all returning `Promise<T | null>`.

- **Loading state**: A single `loading` boolean tracks in-flight requests.

Try again later.' },\n});\n\n/**\n * Admin auth middleware.\n * 1. Checks Firebase Admin SDK is initialized (503 if not)\n * 2. Extracts Bearer token from Authorization header (401 if missing)\n * 3. Calls verifyIdToken(token, true) with checkRevoked=true (401 on failure)\n * 4. Fetches Firestore users/{uid} and checks role === 'admin' (403 if not)\n * 5. Attaches req.adminUser = { uid, email, role }\n * 6. Writes auth failures to adminAuditLog collection (best-effort, never blocks)\n * 7. Calls next()\n */\nexport async function adminAuthMiddleware(\n  req: Request,\n  res: Response,\n  next: NextFunction\n): Promise<void> {\n  if (!isAdminInitialized()) {\n    res.status(503).json({\n      success: false,\n      error: 'Firebase Admin SDK not available. Service account not configured.',\n    });\n    return;\n  }\n\n  const authHeader = req.headers['authorization'];\n\n  if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {\n    await writeAuditLog('missing_token', null, req);\n    res.status(401).json({\n      success: false,\n      error: 'Authorization header required. Use: Authorization: Bearer <token>',\n    });\n    return;\n  }\n\n  const token = authHeader.slice(7);\n  let uid: string;\n  let email: string;\n\n  try {\n    const decodedToken = await getAuth().verifyIdToken(token, true);\n    uid = decodedToken.uid;\n    email = decodedToken.email ?? '';\n  } catch (error) {\n    logger.warn({ err: error }, 'Admin auth: token verification failed');\n    await writeAuditLog('invalid_token', null, req);\n    res.status(401).json({ success: false, error: 'Invalid or expired token.' });\n    return;\n  }\n\n  try {\n    const userDoc = await getFirestore().collection('users').doc(uid).get();\n\n    if (!userDoc.exists) {\n      logger.warn({ uid }, 'Admin auth: user doc not found in Firestore');\n      await writeAuditLog('user_not_found', uid, req);\n      res.status(403).json({ success: false, error: 'Admin access required.' });\n      return;\n    }\n\n    const data = userDoc.data()!;\n    const role: string = data.role ?? 'client';\n\n    if (role !== 'admin') {\n      logger.warn({ uid, role }, 'Admin auth: non-admin user attempted access');\n      await writeAuditLog('not_admin', uid, req);\n      res.status(403).json({ success: false, error: 'Admin access required.' });\n      return;\n    }\n\n    req.adminUser = { uid, email, role };\n    next();\n  } catch (error) {\n    logger.error({ err: error, uid }, 'Admin auth: Firestore role check failed');\n    await writeAuditLog('firestore_error', uid, req);\n    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: 'Authentication check failed.' });\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Best-effort audit log write. Never throws.\n */\nasync function writeAuditLog(\n  reason: string,\n  uid: string | null,\n  req: Request\n): Promise<void> {\n  try {\n    await getFirestore().collection('adminAuditLog').add({\n      event: 'auth_failure',\n      reason,\n      uid,\n      ip: req.ip ?? null,\n      method: req.method,\n      path: req.path,\n      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),\n    });\n  } catch (err) {\n    logger.warn({ err }, 'adminAuthMiddleware: failed to write audit log');\n  }\n}\n```\n\nUse the Write tool to create this file at the exact path specified. Do not modify any other files.\n\n**File path:** `C:\\Users\\Sami\\client-dashboard\\hooks\\useAdminApi.ts`\n\n**Complete file content:**\n\n```typescript\nimport { useState, useCallback } from 'react';\nimport { getAuth } from 'firebase/auth';\nimport { toast } from 'sonner';\n\nconst BASE_URL = '/admin/api';\n\n/** Shape every backend admin route returns */\ninterface ApiResponse<T = unknown> {\n  success: boolean;\n  data?: T;\n  error?: string;\n  meta?: { total: number; hasMore?: boolean; page?: number };\n}\n\n/** What the hook exposes */\ninterface UseAdminApiReturn {\n  loading: boolean;\n  get: <T>(path: string, params?: Record<string, string | number | boolean>) => Promise<T | null>;\n  post: <T>(path: string, body: unknown) => Promise<T | null>;\n  put: <T>(path: string, body: unknown) => Promise<T | null>;\n  patch: <T>(path: string, body: unknown) => Promise<T | null>;\n  del: <T>(path: string, body?: unknown) => Promise<T | null>;\n  bulkDelete: <T>(path: string, ids: string[]) => Promise<T | null>;\n}\n\n/**\n * Shared hook for all Admin CMS API calls.\n *\n * - Automatically injects Firebase ID token as `Authorization: Bearer <token>`\n * - Auto-refreshes expired token (getIdToken handles this natively)\n * - Tracks global loading state\n * - Shows sonner toast on any error\n * - Returns null on error (never throws)\n *\n * Usage:\n * ```tsx\n * const { get, post, del, loading } = useAdminApi();\n * const users = await get<User[]>('/users', { limit: 25, page: 1 });\n * const created = await post<User>('/users', { email: 'a@b.com', role: 'admin' });\n * await del('/users/uid123');\n * await bulkDelete('/users', ['uid1', 'uid2']);\n * ```\n */\nexport function useAdminApi(): UseAdminApiReturn {\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);\n\n  const getToken = useCallback(async (): Promise<string | null> => {\n    const currentUser = getAuth().currentUser;\n    if (!currentUser) {\n      toast.error('Not authenticated. Please sign in.');\n      return null;\n    }\n    try {\n      return await currentUser.getIdToken(false);\n    } catch {\n      toast.error('Session expired. Please sign in again.');\n      return null;\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  const buildHeaders = useCallback(\n    async (includeBody = false): Promise<HeadersInit | null> => {\n      const token = await getToken();\n      if (!token) return null;\n      const headers: HeadersInit = { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` };\n      if (includeBody) headers['Content-Type'] = 'application/json';\n      return headers;\n    },\n    [getToken]\n  );\n\n  const request = useCallback(\n    async <T>(\n      method: string,\n      path: string,\n      body?: unknown,\n      params?: Record<string, string | number | boolean>\n    ): Promise<T | null> => {\n      setLoading(true);\n      try {\n        const headers = await buildHeaders(body !== undefined);\n        if (!headers) return null;\n\n        let url = `${BASE_URL}${path.startsWith('/') ? path : '/' + path}`;\n        if (params && Object.keys(params).length > 0) {\n          const qs = new URLSearchParams(\n            Object.fromEntries(Object.entries(params).map(([k, v]) => [k, String(v)]))\n          ).toString();\n          url += `?${qs}`;\n        }\n\n        const res = await fetch(url, {\n          method,\n          headers,\n          body: body !== undefined ? JSON.stringify(body) : undefined,\n        });\n\n        const json: ApiResponse<T> = await res.json();\n\n        if (!res.ok || !json.success) {\n          const message = json.error ?? `Request failed: ${res.status} ${res.statusText}`;\n          toast.error(message);\n          return null;\n        }\n\n        return (json.data ?? null) as T | null;\n      } catch (err) {\n        toast.error(err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Network error');\n        return null;\n      } finally {\n        setLoading(false);\n      }\n    },\n    [buildHeaders]\n  );\n\n  const get = useCallback(\n    <T>(path: string, params?: Record<string, string | number | boolean>) =>\n      request<T>('GET', path, undefined, params),\n    [request]\n  );\n\n  const post = useCallback(\n    <T>(path: string, body: unknown) => request<T>('POST', path, body),\n    [request]\n  );\n\n  const put = useCallback(\n    <T>(path: string, body: unknown) => request<T>('PUT', path, body),\n    [request]\n  );\n\n  const patch = useCallback(\n    <T>(path: string, body: unknown) => request<T>('PATCH', path, body),\n    [request]\n  );\n\n  const del = useCallback(\n    <T>(path: string, body?: unknown) => request<T>('DELETE', path, body),\n    [request]\n  );\n\n  const bulkDelete = useCallback(\n    <T>(path: string, ids: string[]) => request<T>('DELETE', path, { ids }),\n    [request]\n  );\n\n  return { loading, get, post, put, patch, del, bulkDelete };\n}\n```\n\nUse the Write tool to create this file at the exact path specified. That's all — one file, done."}

Input: {
  "file_path": "C:\\Users\\Sami\\client-dashboard\\hooks\\useAdminApi.ts"

ASSISTANT:      1→import { useState, useCallback } from 'react';
     2→import { getAuth } from 'firebase/auth';
     3→import { toast } from 'sonner';
     4→
     5→const BASE_URL = '/admin/api';
     6→
     7→/** Shape every backend admin route returns */
     8→interface ApiResponse<T = unknown> {
     9→  success: boolean;
    10→  data?: T;
    11→  error?: string;
    12→  meta?: { total: number; hasMore?: boolean; page?: number };
    13→}
    14→
    15→/** What the hook exposes */
    16→interface UseAdminApiReturn {
    17→  loading: boolean;
    18→  get: <T>(path: string, params?: Record<string, string | number | boolean>) => Promise<T | null>;
    19→  post: <T>(path: string, body: unknown) => Promise<T | null>;
    20→  put: <T>(path: string, body: unknown) => Promise<T | null>;
    21→  patch: <T>(path: string, body: unknown) => Promise<T | null>;
    22→  del: <T>(path: string, body?: unknown) => Promise<T | null>;
    23→  bulkDelete: <T>(path: string, ids: string[]) => Promise<T | null>;
    24→}
    25→
    26→/**
    27→ * Shared hook for all Admin CMS API calls.
    28→ *
    29→ * - Automatically injects Firebase ID token as `Authorization: Bearer <token>`
    30→ * - Auto-refreshes expired token (getIdToken handles this natively)
    31→ * - Tracks global loading state
    32→ * - Shows sonner toast on any error
    33→ * - Returns null on error (never throws)
    34→ *
    35→ * Usage:
    36→ * ```tsx
    37→ * const { get, post, del, loading } = useAdminApi();
    38→ * const users = await get<User[]>('/users', { limit: 25, page: 1 });
    39→ * const created = await post<User>('/users', { email: 'a@b.com', role: 'admin' });
    40→ * await del('/users/uid123');
    41→ * await bulkDelete('/users', ['uid1', 'uid2']);
    42→ * ```
    43→ */
    44→export function useAdminApi(): UseAdminApiReturn {
    45→  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
    46→
    47→  const getToken = useCallback(async (): Promise<string | null> => {
    48→    const currentUser = getAuth().currentUser;
    49→    if (!currentUser) {
    50→      toast.error('Not authenticated. Please sign in.');
    51→      return null;
    52→    }
    53→    try {
    54→      return await currentUser.getIdToken(false);
    55→    } catch {
    56→      toast.error('Session expired. Please sign in again.');
    57→      return null;
    58→    }
    59→  }, []);
    60→
    61→  const buildHeaders = useCallback(
    62→    async (includeBody = false): Promise<HeadersInit | null> => {
    63→      const token = await getToken();
    64→      if (!token) return null;
    65→      const headers: HeadersInit = { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` };
    66→      if (includeBody) headers['Content-Type'] = 'application/json';
    67→      return headers;
    68→    },
    69→    [getToken]
    70→  );
    71→
    72→  const request = useCallback(
    73→    async <T>(
    74→      method: string,
    75→      path: string,
    76→      body?: unknown,
    77→      params?: Record<string, string | number | boolean>
    78→    ): Promise<T | null> => {
    79→      setLoading(true);
    80→      try {
    81→        const headers = await buildHeaders(body !== undefined);
    82→        if (!headers) return null;
    83→
    84→        let url = `${BASE_URL}${path.startsWith('/') ? path : '/' + path}`;
    85→        if (params && Object.keys(params).length > 0) {
    86→          const qs = new URLSearchParams(
    87→            Object.fromEntries(Object.entries(params).map(([k, v]) => [k, String(v)]))
    88→          ).toString();
    89→          url += `?${qs}`;
    90→        }
    91→
    92→        const res = await fetch(url, {
    93→          method,
    94→          headers,
    95→          body: body !== undefined ? JSON.stringify(body) : undefined,
    96→        });
    97→
    98→        const json: ApiResponse<T> = await res.json();
    99→
   100→        if (!res.ok || !json.success) {
   101→          const message = json.error ?? `Request failed: ${res.status} ${res.statusText}`;
   102→          toast.error(message);
   103→          return null;
   104→        }
   105→
   106→        return (json.data ?? null) as T | null;
   107→      } catch (err) {
   108→        toast.error(err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Network error');
   109→        return null;
   110→      } finally {
   111→        setLoading(false);
   112→      }
   113→    },
   114→    [buildHeaders]
   115→  );
   116→
   117→  const get = useCallback(
   118→    <T>(path: string, params?: Record<string, string | number | boolean>) =>
   119→      request<T>('GET', path, undefined, params),
   120→    [request]
   121→  );
   122→
   123→  const post = useCallback(
   124→    <T>(path: string, body: unknown) => request<T>('POST', path, body),
   125→    [request]
   126→  );
   127→
   128→  const put = useCallback(
   129→    <T>(path: string, body: unknown) => request<T>('PUT', path, body),
   130→    [request]
   131→  );
   132→
   133→  const patch = useCallback(
   134→    <T>(path: string, body: unknown) => request<T>('PATCH', path, body),
   135→    [request]
   136→  );
   137→
   138→  const del = useCallback(
   139→    <T>(path: string, body?: unknown) => request<T>('DELETE', path, body),
   140→    [request]
   141→  );
   142→
   143→  const bulkDelete = useCallback(
   144→    <T>(path: string, ids: string[]) => request<T>('DELETE', path, { ids }),
   145→    [request]
   146→  );
   147→
   148→  return { loading, get, post, put, patch, del, bulkDelete };
   149→}
   150→

Math.ceil(totalCount / pageSize)\n    : table.getPageCount();\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"flex flex-col gap-3\">\n\n      {/* Toolbar */}\n      <div className=\"flex items-center gap-3 border-border-color rounded-lg text-text-primary placeholder:text-text-secondary focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-primary\"\n          />\n          {filterValue && (\n            <button\n              onClick={() => handleFilterChange('')}\n              className=\"absolute right-2 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-text-secondary hover:text-text-primary\"\n              aria-label=\"Clear          <button\n            onClick={() => setVisibilityOpen((v) => !v)}\n            className=\"flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-2 text-sm bg-glass border border-border-color rounded-lg text-text-secondary hover:text-text-primary transition-colors\"\n            aria-label=\"Toggle column visibility\"\n            aria-expanded={visibilityOpen}\n          >\n            <Columns className=\"h-4 w-4\" />\n            Columns\n          </button>\n          {visibilityOpen && (\n            <div className=\"absolute right-0 top-full mt-1 z-50 bg-glass border border-border-color type=\"checkbox\"\n                      checked={col.getIsVisible()}\n                      onChange={col.getToggleVisibilityHandler()}\n                      className=\"h-3.5 w-3.5 accent-primary\"\n                    />\n                    {typeof col.columnDef.header === 'string' ? col.columnDef.header : col.id}\n                  </label>\n                ))}\n            </div>\n          )}\n        </div>\n\n        {/* Export CSV */}\n        <button\n          onClick={handleExportCSV}\n          className=\"flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-2 text-sm bg-glass border border-border-color rounded-lg text-text-secondary hover:text-text-primary transition-colors\"\n          aria-label=\"Export to CSV\"\n        >\n          <Download className=\"h-4 w-4\" />\n          Export\n        </button>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Table */}\n      <div className=\"overflow-x-auto rounded-xl border border-border-color\">\n        <table className=\"w-full text-sm\" bg-glass-light\">\n                {hg.headers.map((header) => {\n                  const sorted = header.column.getIsSorted();\n                  return (\n                    <th\n                      key={header.id}\n                      scope=\"col\"\n                      style={{ width: header.getSize() !== 150 ? header.getSize() : undefined }}\n                      className=\"px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-semibold text-text-secondary uppercase tracking-wider select-none\"\n                      aria-sort={sorted === 'asc' ? 'ascending' : sorted === 'desc' ? 'descending' : 'none'}\n                    >\n                      {header.isPlaceholder ? null : (\n                        <div\n                          className={`flex items-center gap-1 ${header.column.getCanSort() ? 'cursor-pointer hover:text-text-primary' : ''}`}\n                          onClick={header.column.getToggleSortingHandler()}\n                        >\n                          {flexRender(header.column.columnDef.header, header.getContext())}\n                          {header.column.getCanSort() && (\n                            <span className=\"text-text-secondary\">\n                              {sorted === 'asc' ? (\n                                <ChevronUp className=\"h-3.5 w-3.5\" />\n                              ) : sorted === 'desc' ? (\n                                <ChevronDown className=\"h-3.5 w-3.5\" />\n                              ) : (\n                                <ChevronsUpDown className=\"h-3.5 w-3.5 opacity-40\" />\n                              )}\n                            </span>\n                          )}\n                        </div>\n                      )}\n                    </th>\n                  );\n                })}\n              </tr>\n            ))}\n          </thead>\n          <tbody>\n            {isLoading ? onPageChange(controlledPageIndex + 1) : table.nextPage()}\n            disabled={controlledPageIndex + 1 >= (totalPages || 1)}\n            className=\"p-1.5 rounded-lg border border-border-color bg-glass hover:bg-glass-light disabled:opacity-40 disabled:cursor-not-allowed transition-colors\"\n            aria-label=\"Next page\"\n          >\n            <ChevronRight className=\"h-4 w-4\" />\n          </button>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Floating bulk action bar */}\n      {hasSelection && bulkActions.length > 0 && (\n        <div\n          role=\"toolbar\"\n          aria-label=\"Bulk actions\"\n          className=\"fixed bottom-6 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 z-50 flex items-center gap-3 px-5 py-3 bg-glass border border-border-color rounded-2xl shadow-2xl backdrop-blur-md\"\n        >\n          <span className=\"text-sm font-medium text-text-primary mr-2\">\n            {selectedIds.length} selected\n          </span>\n          {bulkActions.map((action) => (\n            <button\n              key={action.label}\n              onClick={() => action.onClick(selectedIds)}\n              className={`px-4 py-1.5 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium transition-colors ${\n                action.variant === 'danger'\n                  ? 'bg-red-500/10 text-red-400 hover:bg-red-500/20 border border-red-500/30'\n                  : 'bg-primary text-white hover:bg-primary/90'\n              }`}\n            >\n              {action.label}\n            </button>\n          ))}\n          <button\n            onClick={() => setRowSelection({})}\n            className=\"ml-1 text-text-secondary hover:text-text-primary\"\n            aria-label=\"Clear selection\"\n          >\n            <X className=\"h-4 w-4\" />\n          </button>\n        </div>\n      )}\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n```\n\nThat is the complete file. './schemas/userSchemas';\n\nconst router = Router();\n\n// ─── Helper: write to adminAuditLog (best-effort) ────────────────────────────\n\nasync function auditLog(\n  adminUid: string,\n  actionType: ─── GET /users — paginated list with search/filter ──────────────────────────\n// Query params: limit, startAfter, role, status, search\n\nrouter.get('/', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {\n const { limit, startAfter, role, status, search } = query.data;\n\n    let q = getFirestore().collection('users').orderBy('email').limit(limit);\n\n    if (role) q = q.where('role', '==', role) as '').toLowerCase().includes(s)\n      );\n    }\n\n    // Total count (approximate — full collection without filters)\n    const countSnap = await getFirestore().collection('users').count().get();\n    const total = countSnap.data().count;\n\n    res.json({\n      success: true,\n      data: users,\n      meta: {\n        total,\n        hasMore: snapshot.docs.length === limit,\n        nextCursor: snapshot.docs.length === limit ? // NOTE: \"if\" is valid as a Firestore field key even though it's a JS keyword\n  paymenterUserId?: number;\n}\n```\n\n```ts\nimport { Router, Request, Response } from 'express';\nimport { getFirestore } from './firebaseAdmin';\nimport logger from './logger';\nimport {\n  createClientSchema,\n  updateClientSchema,\n  listClientsQuerySchema,\n} from './schemas/clientSchemas';\n\nconst router = Router();\n\n// ─── Helper: audit log (best-effort) ─────────────────────────────────────────\n\nasync function auditLog(\n  adminUid: string,\n  actionType: string,\n  entityId: string,\n  details: Record<string, unknown> = {}\n) {\n  try {\n    await getFirestore().collection('adminAuditLog').add({\n      adminUserId: adminUid,\n      entityType: 'client',\n      actionType,\n      entityId,\n      details,\n      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),\n    });\n  } catch (err) {\n    logger.warn({ err }, 'Client auditLog write failed');\n  }\n}\n\n// ─── GET /clients — paginated list ───────────────────────────────────────────\n\nrouter.get('/', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {\n  try {\n    const query = listClientsQuerySchema.safeParse(req.query);\n    if (!query.success) {\n      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: query.error.errors[0].message });\n    }\n    const { limit, startAfter, userId, search } = query.data;\n\n    let q = getFirestore().collection('clients').orderBy('name').limit(limit) as any;\n    if (userId) q = q.where('userId', '==', userId);\n    if (startAfter) {\n      const cursorDoc = await getFirestore().collection('clients').doc(startAfter).get();\n      if (cursorDoc.exists) q = q.startAfter(cursorDoc);\n    }\n\n    const snapshot = await q.get();\n    let clients = snapshot.docs.map((d: any) => ({ id: d.id, ...d.data() }));\n\n    if (search) {\n      const s = search.toLowerCase();\n      clients = clients.filter((c: any) =>\n        (c.name ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(s) ||\n        (c.ice ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(s) ||\n        (c.rc ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(s)\n      );\n    }\n\n    const countSnap = await getFirestore().collection('clients').count().get();\n    const total = countSnap.data().count;\n\n    res.json({\n      success: true,\n      data: clients,\n      meta: {\n        total,\n        hasMore: snapshot.docs.length === limit,\n        nextCursor: snapshot.docs.length === limit ? snapshot.docs[snapshot.docs.length - 1].id : null,\n      },\n    });\n  } catch (error) {\n    logger.error({ err: error }, 'GET /clients failed');\n    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: 'Failed to list clients' });\n  }\n});\n\n// ─── GET /clients/:id ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nrouter.get('/:id', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {\n  try {\n    const doc = await getFirestore().collection('clients').doc(req.params.id).get();\n    if (!doc.exists) return res.status(404).json({ success: false, error: 'Client not found' });\n    res.json({ success: true, data: { id: doc.id, ...doc.data() } });\n  } catch (error) {\n    logger.error({ err: error }, 'GET /clients/:id failed');\n    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: 'Failed to get client' });\n  }\n});\n\n// ─── POST /clients — create with unique rc/ice check ─────────────────────────\n\nrouter.post('/', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {\n  try {\n    const parsed = createClientSchema.safeParse(req.body);\n    if (!parsed.success) {\n      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: parsed.error.errors[0].message });\n    }\n    const data = parsed.data;\n    const db = getFirestore();\n\n    // Unique rc check\n    const rcSnap = await db.collection('clients').where('rc', '==', data.rc).limit(1).get();\n    if (!rcSnap.empty) {\n      return res.status(409).json({ success: false, error: `A client with RC \"${data.rc}\" already exists` });\n    }\n    // Unique ice check\n    const iceSnap = await db.collection('clients').where('ice', '==', data.ice).limit(1).get();\n    if (!iceSnap.empty) {\n      return res.status(409).json({ success: false, error: `A client with ICE \"${data.ice}\" already exists` });\n    }\n\n    const docRef = await db.collection('clients').add({\n      ...data,\n      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),\n      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),\n    });\n\n    const adminUid = (req as any).adminUser?.uid ?? 'system';\n    await auditLog(adminUid, 'create', docRef.id, { name: data.name });\n\n    res.status(201).json({ success: true, data: { id: docRef.id, ...data } });\n  } catch (error) {\n    logger.error({ err: error }, 'POST /clients failed');\n    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to create client' });\n  }\n});\n\n// ─── PUT /clients/:id ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nrouter.put('/:id', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {\n  try {\n    const { id } = req.params;\n    const parsed = updateClientSchema.safeParse(req.body);\n    if (!parsed.success) {\n      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: parsed.error.errors[0].message });\n    }\n    const data = parsed.data;\n    const db = getFirestore();\n\n    const existing = await db.collection('clients').doc(id).get();\n    if (!existing.exists) return res.status(404).json({ success: false, error: 'Client not found' });\n\n    await db.collection('clients').doc(id).update({ ...data, updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() });\n\n    const adminUid = (req as any).adminUser?.uid ?? 'system';\n    await auditLog(adminUid, 'update', id, data as Record<string, unknown>);\n\n    res.json({ success: true, data: { id, ...existing.data(), ...data } });\n  } catch (error) {\n    logger.error({ err: error }, 'PUT /clients/:id failed');\n    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: 'Failed to update client' });\n  }\n});\n\n// ─── DELETE /clients/:id ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nrouter.delete('/:id', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {\n  try {\n    const { id } = req.params;\n    const db = getFirestore();\n    const doc = await db.collection('clients').doc(id).get();\n    if (!doc.exists) return res.status(404).json({ success: false, error: 'Client not found' });\n    await db.collection('clients').doc(id).delete();\n    const adminUid = (req as any).adminUser?.uid ?? 'system';\n    await auditLog(adminUid, 'delete', id);\n    res.json({ success: true, data: { id, deleted: true } });\n  } catch (error) {\n    logger.error({ err: error }, 'DELETE /clients/:id failed');\n    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: 'Failed to delete client' });\n  }\n});\n\n// ─── GET /clients/export/csv — export all as CSV ─────────────────────────────\n\nrouter.get('/export/csv', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {\n  try {\n    const snapshot = await getFirestore().collection('clients').orderBy('name').get();\n    const clients = snapshot.docs.map((d) => ({ id: d.id, ...d.data() })) as any[];\n\n    const fields = ['id', 'name', 'ice', 'rc', 'if', 'adresse', 'adresse2', 'userId', 'brandId', 'paymenterUserId'];\n    const header = fields.join(',');\n    const rows = clients.map((c) =>\n      fields.map((f) => {\n        const v = c[f] ?? '';\n        return `\"${String(v).replace(/\"/g, '\"\"')}\"`;\n      }).join(',')\n    );\n    const csv = [header, ...rows].join('\\n');\n\n    res.setHeader('Content-Type', 'text/csv');\n    res.setHeader('Content-Disposition', 'attachment; filename=\"clients.csv\"');\n    res.send(csv);\n  } catch (error) {\n    logger.error({ err: error }, 'GET /clients/export/csv failed');\n    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: 'CSV export failed' });\n  }\n});\n\nexport default router;\n```\n\nWrite BOTH files to their exact paths. ─── GET /users — paginated list with search/filter ──────────────────────────\n// Query params: limit, startAfter, role, status, search\n\nrouter.get('/', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {\n
