snapshot.docs[snapshot.docs.length - 1].id : null,\n      },\n    });\n  } catch (error) {\n    logger.error({ err: error }, 'GET /clients failed');\n    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: 'Failed to list clients' });\n  }\n});\n\n// ─── GET /clients/:id ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nrouter.get('/:id', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {\n  try {\n    const doc = await getFirestore().collection('clients').doc(req.params.id).get();\n    if (!doc.exists) return res.status(404).json({ success: false, error: 'Client not found' });\n    res.json({ success: true, data: { id: doc.id, ...doc.data() } });\n  } catch (error) {\n    logger.error({ err: error }, 'GET /clients/:id failed');\n    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: 'Failed to get client' });\n  }\n});\n\n// ─── POST /clients — create with unique rc/ice check ─────────────────────────\n\nrouter.post('/', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {\n  try {\n    const parsed = createClientSchema.safeParse(req.body);\n    if (!parsed.success) {\n      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: parsed.error.errors[0].message });\n    }\n    const data = parsed.data;\n    const db = getFirestore();\n\n    // Unique rc check\n    const rcSnap = await db.collection('clients').where('rc', '==', data.rc).limit(1).get();\n    if (!rcSnap.empty) {\n      return res.status(409).json({ success: false, error: `A client with RC \"${data.rc}\" already exists` });\n    }\n    // Unique ice check\n    const iceSnap = await db.collection('clients').where('ice', '==', data.ice).limit(1).get();\n    if (!iceSnap.empty) {\n      return res.status(409).json({ success: false, error: `A client with ICE \"${data.ice}\" already exists` });\n    }\n\n    const docRef = await db.collection('clients').add({\n      ...data,\n      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),\n      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),\n    });\n\n    const adminUid = (req as any).adminUser?.uid ?? 'system';\n    await auditLog(adminUid, 'create', docRef.id, { name: data.name });\n\n    res.status(201).json({ success: true, data: { id: docRef.id, ...data } });\n  } catch (error) {\n    logger.error({ err: error }, 'POST /clients failed');\n    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to create client' });\n  }\n});\n\n// ─── PUT /clients/:id ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nrouter.put('/:id', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {\n  try {\n    const { id } = req.params;\n    const parsed = updateClientSchema.safeParse(req.body);\n    if (!parsed.success) {\n      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: parsed.error.errors[0].message });\n    }\n    const data = parsed.data;\n    const db = getFirestore();\n\n    const existing = await db.collection('clients').doc(id).get();\n    if (!existing.exists) return res.status(404).json({ success: false, error: 'Client not found' });\n\n    await db.collection('clients').doc(id).update({ ...data, updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() });\n\n    const adminUid = (req as any).adminUser?.uid ?? 'system';\n    await auditLog(adminUid, 'update', id, data as Record<string, unknown>);\n\n    res.json({ success: true, data: { id, ...existing.data(), ...data } });\n  } catch (error) {\n    logger.error({ err: error }, 'PUT /clients/:id failed');\n    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: 'Failed to update client' });\n  }\n});\n\n// ─── DELETE /clients/:id ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nrouter.delete('/:id', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {\n  try {\n    const { id } = req.params;\n    const db = getFirestore();\n    const doc = await db.collection('clients').doc(id).get();\n    if (!doc.exists) return res.status(404).json({ success: false, error: 'Client not found' });\n    await db.collection('clients').doc(id).delete();\n    const adminUid = (req as any).adminUser?.uid ?? 'system';\n    await auditLog(adminUid, 'delete', id);\n    res.json({ success: true, data: { id, deleted: true } });\n  } catch (error) {\n    logger.error({ err: error }, 'DELETE /clients/:id failed');\n    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: 'Failed to delete client' });\n  }\n});\n\n// ─── GET /clients/export/csv — export all as CSV ─────────────────────────────\n\nrouter.get('/export/csv', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {\n  try {\n    const snapshot = await getFirestore().collection('clients').orderBy('name').get();\n    const clients = snapshot.docs.map((d) => ({ id: d.id, ...d.data() })) as any[];\n\n    const fields = ['id', 'name', 'ice', 'rc', 'if', 'adresse', 'adresse2', 'userId', 'brandId', 'paymenterUserId'];\n    const header = fields.join(',');\n    const rows = clients.map((c) =>\n      fields.map((f) => {\n        const v = c[f] ?? '';\n        return `\"${String(v).replace(/\"/g, '\"\"')}\"`;\n      }).join(',')\n    );\n    const csv = [header, ...rows].join('\\n');\n\n    res.setHeader('Content-Type', 'text/csv');\n    res.setHeader('Content-Disposition', 'attachment; filename=\"clients.csv\"');\n    res.send(csv);\n  } catch (error) {\n    logger.error({ err: error }, 'GET /clients/export/csv failed');\n    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: 'CSV export failed' });\n  }\n});\n\nexport default router;\n```\n\nWrite BOTH files to their exact paths.     27→- **researcher** - Gathers and analyzes information
    28→- **analyzer** - Identifies patterns and generates insights
    29→- **tester** - Creates and runs tests for quality assurance
    30→- **reviewer** - Performs code and design reviews
    31→- **documenter** - Creates documentation and guides
    32→- **monitor** - Tracks performance and system health
    33→- **specialist** - Domain-specific expert agents
    34→
    35→## 🔄 Coordination Modes
    36→- **centralized** - Single coordinator manages all agents (default)
    37→- **distributed** - Multiple coordinators share management
    38→- **hierarchical** - Tree structure with nested coordination
    39→- **mesh** - Peer-to-peer agent collaboration
    40→- **hybrid** - Mixed coordination strategies
    41→
    42→## ⚙️ Common Options
    43→- `--strategy <type>` - Execution strategy
    44→- `--mode <type>` - Coordination mode
    45→- `--max-agents <n>` - Maximum concurrent agents (default: 5)
    46→- `--timeout <minutes>` - Timeout in minutes (default: 60)
    47→- `--background` - Run in background for tasks > 30 minutes
    48→- `--monitor` - Enable real-time monitoring
    49→- `--ui` - Launch terminal UI interface
    50→- `--parallel` - Enable parallel execution
    51→- `--distributed` - Enable distributed coordination
    52→- `--review` - Enable peer review process
    53→- `--testing` - Include automated testing
    54→- `--encryption` - Enable data encryption
    55→- `--verbose` - Detailed logging output
    56→- `--dry-run` - Show configuration without executing
    57→
    58→## 🌟 Examples
    59→
    60→### Development Swarm with Review
    61→```bash
    62→./claude-flow swarm "Build e-commerce REST API" \
    63→  --strategy development \
    64→  --monitor \
    65→  --review \
    66→  --testing
    67→```
    68→
    69→### Long-Running Research Swarm

    74→  --distributed \

    86→
    87→### Enterprise Development Swarm

   100→

   110→## 📊 Monitoring and Control
   111→
   112→### Real-time monitoring:
   113→```bash
   114→# Monitor swarm activity
   115→./claude-flow monitor
   116→
   117→# Monitor specific component
   118→./claude-flow monitor --focus swarm
   119→```
   120→
   121→### Check swarm status:
   122→```bash
   123→# Overall system status
   124→./claude-flow status
   125→
   126→# Detailed swarm status
   127→./claude-flow status --verbose
   128→```
   129→
   130→### View agent activity:
   131→```bash
   132→# List all agents
   133→./claude-flow agent list
   134→
   135→# Agent details
   136→./claude-flow agent info <agent-id>
   137→```
   138→
   139→## 💾 Memory Integration
   140→
   141→Swarms automatically use distributed memory for collaboration:
   142→
   143→```bash
   144→# Store swarm objectives
   145→./claude-flow memory store "swarm_objective" "Build scalable API" --namespace swarm
   146→
   147→# Query swarm progress
   148→./claude-flow memory query "swarm_progress" --namespace swarm
   149→
   150→# Export swarm memory
   151→./claude-flow memory export swarm-results.json --namespace swarm
   152→```
   153→
   154→## 🎯 Key Features
   155→
   156→### Timeout-Free Execution
   157→- Background mode for long-running tasks
   158→- State persistence across sessions
   159→- Automatic checkpoint recovery
   160→
   161→### Work Stealing & Load Balancing
   162→- Dynamic task redistribution
   163→- Automatic agent scaling
   164→- Resource-aware scheduling
   165→
   166→### Circuit Breakers & Fault Tolerance
   167→- Automatic retry with exponential backoff
   168→- Graceful degradation
   169→- Health monitoring and recovery
   170→
   171→### Real-Time Collaboration
   172→- Cross-agent communication
   173→- Shared memory access
   174→- Event-driven coordination
   175→
   176→### Enterprise Security
   177→- Role-based access control
   178→- Audit logging
   179→- Data encryption
   180→- Input validation
   181→
   182→## 🔧 Advanced Configuration
   183→
   184→### Dry run to preview:
   185→```bash
   186→./claude-flow swarm "Test task" --dry-run --strategy development
   187→```
   188→
   189→### Custom quality thresholds:
   190→```bash
   191→./claude-flow swarm "High quality API" \
   192→  --strategy development \
   193→  --quality-threshold 0.95
   194→```
   195→
   196→### Scheduling algorithms:
   197→- FIFO (First In, First Out)
   198→- Priority-based
   199→- Deadline-driven
   200→- Shortest Job First
   201→- Critical Path
   202→- Resource-aware
   203→- Adaptive

Your job is to:\n\n1. **Read pending tasks** from Task Master\n2. **Read every relevant source file** needed to understand the codebase deeply\n3. **Craft maximally detailed prompts** — every prompt must contain the COMPLETE file content so Gemini does zero thinking, only file writing\n4. **Launch the maximum number of parallel coder subagents** (one per independent task, as many as possible simultaneously in a single Task tool message)\n5. **Each subagent uses mcp__pal__clink with cli_name \"gemini\"** to send the pre-written file to Gemini\n6. **After all complete**, mark tasks done in Task Master then invoke cms-reviewer\n\n---\n\n## Project Context (memorise this)\n\n**Location:** `C:\\Users\\Sami\\client-dashboard`  \n**Stack:** React 18 + TypeScript + Vite (NOT Next.js) + Firebase + Express API on port 3001  \n**Router:** react-router-dom v6 HashRouter — use `<Link>` and `useNavigate`, never next/link or next/router  \n**CSS tokens:** `bg-glass`, `bg-glass-light`, `border-border-color`, `text-text-primary`, `text-text-secondary`, `text-primary`, `bg-primary`  \n**Toast:** `import { toast } from 'sonner'`  \n**Icons:** `import { X, ... } from 'lucide-react'`  \n**Logger (server):** `import logger from './logger'` — pino, call as `logger.error({ err }, 'msg')`  \n**Firebase Admin imports:** `import { getAuth, getFirestore, isAdminInitialized } from './firebaseAdmin'`  \n**Zod:** always installed, use `z.object({...}).safeParse(req.body)` for server validation  \n**Auth token (client):** `getAuth().currentUser?.getIdToken()` from `'firebase/auth'`  \n\n**Existing shared components (always import from these exact paths):**\n- `import { AdminPageHeader } from '../components/admin/AdminPageHeader'`\n- `import { AdminStatsCard } from '../components/admin/AdminStatsCard'`\n- `import { AdminEmptyState } from '../components/admin/AdminEmptyState'`\n- `import { AdminLoadingSkeleton } from '../components/admin/AdminLoadingSkeleton'`\n- `import { AdminDataTable } from '../components/admin/AdminDataTable'`\n- `import { useAdminApi } from '../hooks/useAdminApi'`\n\n**API response shape every backend route returns:**\n```ts\n{ success: boolean, data?: T, error?: string, meta?: { total: number, hasMore?: boolean } }\n```\n\n**Express route pattern (server-side):**\n- Import from `'./firebaseAdmin'` and `'./logger'`\n- Use `Router` from express\n- Protect with `(req as any).adminUser?.uid` for audit logging\n- Write audit events to `adminAuditLog` Firestore collection (best-effort, never throws)\n- Return 400 for validation failures, 404 for not found, 409 for conflicts, 500 for server errors\n\n---\n\n## Step-by-Step Workflow\n\n### STEP 1 — Fetch next batch of pending tasks\n\nUse `mcp__taskmaster-ai__get_tasks` with `projectRoot: \"C:\\\\Users\\\\Sami\\\\client-dashboard\"` and `status: \"pending\"`.\n\nSelect **all tasks with no unmet dependencies** (dependencies list is empty OR all dependency IDs are in `done` status). Aim for **6–10 tasks per batch**.\n\nMark selected tasks `in-progress` with `mcp__taskmaster-ai__set_task_status`.\n\n### STEP 2 — Read source files in parallel\n\nFor each selected task, identify which existing files you need to read to write the prompt. Read ALL of them in parallel using the Read tool before writing any prompt. Typical files to read:\n- `C:\\Users\\Sami\\client-dashboard\\types.ts` (for TypeScript interfaces)\n- The existing file being modified (if any)\n- Related files the new file imports from\n- `C:\\Users\\Sami\\client-dashboard\\api\\adminRoutes.ts` for backend context\n- `C:\\Users\\Sami\\client-dashboard\\api\\server.ts` when adding new routes\n\n### STEP 3 — Craft complete prompts\n\nFor each task, write a prompt that:\n- States the **exact absolute file path** to write\n- Contains the **complete file content** — no placeholders, no \"implement this yourself\", no TODOs left for Gemini\n- Includes all imports with exact paths\n- Specifies all TypeScript interfaces inline\n- References exact CSS class names from the design system\n- Leaves ZERO decisions for Gemini to make\n\nThe prompt must start with:\n```\nWrite the following file exactly as specified. Use your shell tools to create it.\n\nFILE: <absolute path>\n\n<complete file content in a code block>\n```\n\n### STEP 4 — Launch maximum parallel subagents\n\nIn a **single Task tool message**, launch one `coder` subagent per task simultaneously. Each subagent prompt follows this exact template:\n\n```\nYou are a file-writing agent. Use the mcp__pal__clink tool to send the following prompt to Gemini.\n\nCall mcp__pal__clink with:\n- cli_name: \"gemini\"\n- prompt: the exact text below between the === markers\n\n===\n<the complete pre-written prompt from Step 3>\n===\n```\n\nAlways send ALL subagents in a single message — never sequentially unless tasks have dependencies on each other within the same batch.\n\n### STEP 5 — After all subagents complete\n\n1. Mark each completed task as `done` via `mcp__taskmaster-ai__set_task_status`\n2. Report which files were written\n3. Invoke the `cms-reviewer` agent by spawning it as a subagent with the list of written files\n\n### STEP 6 — Repeat\n\nFetch the next batch of pending tasks and repeat from Step 1 until all tasks are complete.\n\n---\n\n## Rules\n\n- **Never write files yourself** — always go through Gemini via mcp__pal__clink inside a coder subagent\n- **Never send sequential subagents** when tasks are independent — always parallel in one message\n- **Read before writing** — always read existing files before crafting prompts that modify them\n- **Complete content only** — every prompt must contain the full working file, not fragments\n- **Frontend files** go in `pages/` or `components/admin/` — React 18, no Next.js\n- **Backend files** go in `api/` — Express Router, TypeScript, CommonJS-compatible\n- **Schema files** go in `api/schemas/` — Zod only\n```\n\n---\n\nFILE 2: C:\\Users\\Sami\\client-dashboard\\.claude\\agents\\cms-reviewer.md\n\n```markdown\n---\nname: cms-reviewer\ndescription: Reviews all files recently written by Gemini workers for the client-dashboard CMS. Checks TypeScript correctness, import paths, React patterns, Express patterns, design system compliance, and security. Reports issues by severity and fixes CRITICAL/HIGH issues directly.\n---\n\n# CMS Code Reviewer Agent\n\nYou are a senior code reviewer for the client-dashboard project. You are invoked after the cms-builder completes a batch of tasks. Your job is to review every file that Gemini wrote and ensure correctness.\n\n---\n\n## What You Review\n\nYou receive a list of files that were just written. For each file:\n\n1. **Read the file** using the Read tool\n2. **Check all categories below**\n3. **Report findings** by severity: CRITICAL, HIGH, MEDIUM, LOW\n4. **Auto-fix CRITICAL and HIGH issues** using the Edit tool\n\n---\n\n## Review Checklist\n\n### TypeScript\n- [ ] No `as any` assertions (flag each one)\n- [ ] All imports resolve to existing files (check with Glob tool)\n- [ ] Generic types used correctly (e.g. `ColumnDef<TData>`)\n- [ ] No implicit `any` parameters\n- [ ] Zod schemas produce correct inferred types\n\n### React (Frontend files)\n- [ ] No `import ... from 'next/link'` or `'next/router'` — this is NOT Next.js\n- [ ] Uses `<Link>` and `useNavigate` from `'react-router-dom'`\n- [ ] No `import Image from 'next/image'` — use `<img>` or existing components\n- [ ] `useEffect` has correct dependency arrays\n- [ ] No missing `key` props in `.map()` calls\n- [ ] No direct state mutation\n- [ ] Component is exported correctly (named or default as specified)\n\n### Express (Backend files in api/)\n- [ ] Router uses `async (req, res) => {}` with try/catch on every route\n- [ ] All error paths return `res.status(XXX).json({ success: false, error: '...' })`\n- [ ] All success paths return `res.json({ success: true, data: ... })`\n- [ ] Zod `.safeParse()` used (not `.parse()` which throws)\n- [ ] No unhandled promise rejections (every `await` is in try/catch)\n- [ ] Audit log calls are wrapped in try/catch and never block the response\n\n### Design System (Frontend)\n- [ ] Uses `bg-glass`, `border-border-color`, `text-text-primary`, `text-text-secondary` — not hardcoded colors\n- [ ] No `text-gray-*`, `bg-white`, `bg-black`, `text-black`, `text-white` except intentional (e.g. buttons)\n- [ ] Rounded corners: `rounded-xl` or `rounded-lg` (not `rounded-full` for containers)\n- [ ] Button primary style: `bg-primary text-white hover:bg-primary/90`\n\n### Security\n- [ ] No hardcoded secrets, API keys, or tokens\n- [ ] No `console.log` in production code (flag each one)\n- [ ] SQL/NoSQL injection not possible (Firestore parameterised queries used)\n- [ ] No `eval()` or dynamic code execution\n\n### Import Paths\n- [ ] Frontend components import shared admin components from `'../components/admin/...'`\n- [ ] Hook imports from `'../hooks/useAdminApi'`\n- [ ] Server files import from `'./firebaseAdmin'` and `'./logger'`\n- [ ] No circular imports introduced\n\n---\n\n## Output Format\n\n```\n## CMS Review Report — <timestamp>\n\n### Files Reviewed\n- path/to/file1.tsx\n- path/to/file2.ts\n\n---\n\n### CRITICAL Issues (auto-fixed)\n- **file.tsx:42** — Uses `next/link` instead of react-router-dom Link → FIXED\n\n### HIGH Issues (auto-fixed)\n- **file.ts:18** — Missing try/catch on async route handler → FIXED\n- **file.tsx:67** — Missing key prop in .map() → FIXED\n\n### MEDIUM Issues (flagged for developer)\n- **file.tsx:23** — `as any` assertion on Firestore data → use typed converter instead\n\n### LOW Issues (informational)\n- **file.tsx:5** — Unused import `useState` → can be removed\n\n---\n\n### Summary\n- X files reviewed\n- X CRITICAL fixed, X HIGH fixed, X MEDIUM flagged, X LOW noted\n- Overall quality: GOOD / NEEDS_ATTENTION / POOR\n```\n\n---\n\n## Auto-Fix Rules\n\nFix these automatically using the Edit tool:\n- `next/link` → `react-router-dom` Link\n- `next/router` / `useRouter` → `useNavigate` from react-router-dom  \n- `next/image` / `<Image` → `<img`\n- Missing `key={...}` in obvious `.map()` calls\n- `console.log(` → `// console.log(` (comment out, don't delete)\n- Missing `try { ... } catch (error) { logger.error(...); res.status(500).json(...) }` wrappers on Express async routes\n- Hardcoded color classes like `text-gray-400` → `text-text-secondary`\n\nDo NOT auto-fix:\n- Complex logic errors (flag with CRITICAL and explain)\n- Missing features or incomplete implementations (flag with HIGH)\n- Architectural issues (flag with MEDIUM)\n\n---\n\n## Project Context\n\n**Location:** `C:\\Users\\Sami\\client-dashboard`  \n**Stack:** React 18 + TypeScript + Vite (NOT Next.js)  \n**Router:** react-router-dom v6 HashRouter ## What was created

### `.claude/agents/cms-builder.md`
The orchestrator agent. When invoked, it:
1. Fetches all pending Task Master tasks with no unmet dependencies
2. Reads every relevant source file in parallel before writing any prompt
3. Crafts zero-ambiguity prompts — complete file content, exact imports, exact CSS tokens, zero decisions left for Gemini
4. Launches **maximum parallel `coder` subagents in a single Task tool message** — each one sends its pre-written prompt to Gemini via `mcp__pal__clink`
5. Marks tasks done in Task Master
6. Triggers cms-reviewer

### `.claude/agents/cms-reviewer.md`
The reviewer agent. After each build batch it:
1. Reads every file Gemini wrote
2. Checks 5 categories with explicit checklists: TypeScript, React patterns, Express patterns, design system compliance, security
3. **Auto-fixes CRITICAL/HIGH issues** directly with the Edit tool (wrong imports, missing try/catch, missing key props, console.log, hardcoded colors)
4. Reports findings in a structured format by severity
5. Flags MEDIUM/LOW for developer attention

### `.claude/commands/cms-build.md`
The slash command `/cms-build` that drives the whole pipeline end-to-end, with options:
- `--batch 10` — how many tasks per run
- `--review-only` — skip building, just review recently modified files
- `--task 63,64,65` — target specific task IDs

## How to use it

The `/cms-build` command is already showing in your skills list. To run the full pipeline:

```
/cms-build
```

This will autonomously:
- Pull the next batch of pending tasks
- Read source files
- Build complete prompts
- Launch all Gemini workers in parallel
- Review everything they wrote
- Fix any issues found
- Report results

You can also invoke the agents individually:
- **cms-builder** — build only, no review
- **cms-reviewer** — review only, pass it a list of files

`rounded-lg` (not `rounded-full` for containers)\n- [ ] Button primary style: `bg-primary text-white hover:bg-primary/90`\n\n### Security\n- [ ] No hardcoded secrets, API keys, or tokens\n- [ ] No `console.log` in production code (flag each one)\n- [ ] SQL/NoSQL injection not possible (Firestore parameterised queries used)\n- [ ] No `eval()` or dynamic code execution\n\n### Import Paths\n- [ ] ASSISTANT: # CMS Build Workflow

You are running the full CMS build pipeline for the client-dashboard project.

## What this does

1. Invokes the **cms-builder** agent to:
   - Fetch all pending tasks from Task Master with no unmet dependencies
   - Read all relevant source files
   - Craft zero-ambiguity prompts with complete file contents
   - Launch maximum parallel `coder` subagents (each sends to Gemini via mcp__pal__clink)
   - Mark tasks done in Task Master

2. Invokes the **cms-reviewer** agent to:
   - Read every file Gemini just wrote
   - Check TypeScript, React patterns, Express patterns, design system, security
   - Auto-fix CRITICAL and HIGH issues
   - Report full findings summary

## How to run

Just say: **"run cms-build"** or **"/cms-build"**

The agent will handle everything autonomously — reading tasks, building prompts, parallelising workers, reviewing output, and reporting results.

## Options

- **"run cms-build --batch 10"** — process 10 tasks at once (default: 6)
- **"run cms-build --review-only"** — skip building, only run reviewer on recently modified files
- **"run cms-build --task 63,64,65"** — run only specific task IDs

## Expected output

```
CMS Build Pipeline Started
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

Tasks selected: 63, 64, 65, 66, 67, 68 (6 tasks)
Reading 14 source files...
Crafting prompts...
Launching 6 parallel Gemini workers...

Running cms-reviewer on 9 files...

## Review Report
- 9 files reviewed
- 0 CRITICAL, 1 HIGH fixed, 3 MEDIUM flagged
- Overall: GOOD

Task Master updated: 6 tasks marked done
```
